MSS￨F announces￨F a￨F protocol￨F for￨F finding￨F obesity￨F gene￨F

The￨F Mexican￨F Social￨F Security￨F Institute￨F (MSSI)￨F has￨F announced￨F that￨F conducts￨F a￨F research￨F to￨F discover￨F the￨F gene￨F for￨F obesity￨F in￨F children￨F and￨F young￨F people￨F ,￨F called￨F the￨F protocol￨F of￨F &apos;￨F Genetics￨F of￨F obesity￨F in￨F childhood￨F and￨F adolescence￨F &apos;￨F ,￨F which￨F will￨F provide￨F counting￨F on￨F markers￨F associated￨F with￨F overweight￨F .￨F
In￨F a￨F statement￨F ,￨F the￨F head￨F of￨F the￨F Medical￨F Research￨F Unit￨F in￨F Biochemistry￨F of￨F Specialties￨F Hospital￨F ,￨F XXI￨F Century￨F National￨F Medical￨F Center￨F ,￨F Miguel￨F Cruz￨F Lopez￨F ,￨F explained￨F that￨F it￨F was￨F integrated￨F a￨F multidisciplinary￨F team￨F of￨F physicians￨F ,￨F nurses￨F ,￨F nutritionists￨F and￨F social￨F workers￨F .￨F
The￨F team￨F is￨F supported￨F by￨F specialists￨F and￨F graduate￨F students￨F from￨F the￨F National￨F Institute￨F of￨F Public￨F Health￨F (NIPH)￨F and￨F the￨F Centre￨F for￨F Research￨F and￨F Advanced￨F Studies￨F (Cinvestav)￨F National￨F Polytechnic￨F Institute￨F (NPI).￨F
The￨F research￨F invites￨F the￨F population￨F entitled￨F or￨F not￨F ,￨F to￨F participate￨F by￨F going￨F to￨F the￨F participant￨F sport￨F units￨F of￨F the￨F MSSI￨F in￨F the￨F Valley￨F of￨F Mexico￨F ,￨F where￨F there￨F will￨F be￨F carried￨F out￨F the￨F tests￨F to￨F children￨F ,￨F every￨F Saturday￨F from￨F 8:￨F 00￨F o￨F &apos;clock￨F .￨F
He￨F stressed￨F that￨F the￨F protocol￨F started￨F in￨F the￨F Cuauhtémoc￨F sports￨F unit￨F (West￨F Mexico￨F State)￨F and￨F since￨F October￨F 8th￨F ,￨F the￨F activity￨F takes￨F place￨F in￨F the￨F Netzahualcoyotl￨F Sport￨F unit￨F (East￨F State￨F of￨F Mexico).￨F
Once￨F reached￨F the￨F goal￨F of￨F bringing￨F 500￨F to￨F 600￨F children￨F ,￨F the￨F study￨F will￨F continue￨F in￨F the￨F Independence￨F Sport￨F Unit￨F (South￨F the￨F Mexico￨F City)￨F and￨F finally￨F in￨F the￨F Morelos￨F Sports￨F Unit￨F (North￨F the￨F Mexico￨F City).￨F
He￨F explained￨F that￨F the￨F purpose￨F of￨F this￨F research￨F is￨F to￨F understand￨F the￨F components￨F and￨F the￨F importance￨F of￨F genetics￨F in￨F relation￨F to￨F the￨F development￨F of￨F obesity￨F and￨F identify￨F in￨F children￨F and￨F young￨F Mexicans￨F the￨F risk￨F factors￨F for￨F preventing￨F the￨F appearance￨F of￨F chronic￨F degenerative￨F diseases￨F .￨F
On￨F November￨F 14th￨F ,￨F there￨F will￨F be￨F celebrated￨F the￨F World￨F Diabetes￨F Day￨F ,￨F and￨F the￨F goal￨F is￨F to￨F collect￨F three￨F thousand￨F children￨F and￨F young￨F people￨F between￨F 6￨F and￨F 14￨F years￨F ,￨F with￨F the￨F consent￨F and￨F parental￨F supervision￨F for￨F the￨F implementation￨F of￨F specific￨F questionnaires￨F on￨F food￨F .￨F
They￨F will￨F also￨F be￨F asked￨F about￨F physical￨F activity￨F and￨F family￨F hereditary￨F history￨F of￨F disease￨F ,￨F in￨F order￨F to￨F avoid￨F risk￨F factors￨F that￨F give￨F rise￨F to￨F diseases￨F such￨F as￨F diabetes￨F or￨F kidney￨F failure￨F .￨F
He￨F explained￨F that￨F on￨F Saturday￨F to￨F all￨F participants￨F will￨F be￨F applied￨F anthropometric￨F measurements￨F (weight￨F ,￨F height￨F ,￨F and￨F waist￨F circumference),￨F blood￨F pressure￨F measurements￨F ,￨F and￨F determination￨F of￨F glucose￨F ,￨F triglycerides￨F ,￨F cholesterol￨F and￨F insulin￨F and￨F genetic￨F (seeking￨F to￨F identify￨F genes￨F that￨F are￨F associated￨F to￨F childhood￨F obesity).￨F
Cruz￨F Lopez￨F said￨F that￨F this￨F research￨F reflects￨F the￨F concern￨F of￨F health￨F professionals￨F for￨F the￨F alarming￨F weight￨F gain￨F in￨F children￨F .￨F
Health￨F Surveys￨F made￨F between￨F 1999￨F and￨F 2006￨F reported￨F that￨F in￨F only￨F six￨F years￨F there￨F was￨F an￨F increase￨F in￨F the￨F case￨F of￨F the￨F boys￨F ,￨F 77￨F percent￨F were￨F obese￨F ,￨F and￨F 47￨F percent￨F in￨F the￨F case￨F of￨F the￨F girls;￨F in￨F terms￨F of￨F overweight￨F there￨F was￨F also￨F observed￨F a￨F dramatic￨F rise￨F ,￨F &quot;￨F said￨F the￨F specialist￨F of￨F the￨F MSSI￨F .￨F
He￨F said￨F the￨F justification￨F for￨F searching￨F the￨F markers￨F is￨F based￨F on￨F that￨F the￨F population￨F of￨F the￨F country￨F differs￨F from￨F other￨F in￨F its￨F genetic￨F history￨F .￨F
He￨F reported￨F that￨F on￨F average￨F ,￨F the￨F Mexican￨F has￨F a￨F 65￨F percent￨F of￨F American￨F Indian￨F heritage￨F ,￨F 30￨F percent￨F European￨F and￨F five￨F percent￨F African￨F and￨F this￨F condition￨F is￨F reflected￨F in￨F the￨F genes￨F that￨F are￨F associated￨F with￨F diabetes￨F and￨F overweight￨F .￨F
He￨F explained￨F that￨F generally￨F ,￨F the￨F genetics￨F of￨F obesity￨F result￨F in￨F the￨F inability￨F to￨F burn￨F off￨F the￨F excess￨F energy￨F that￨F we￨F consume￨F (calories)￨F and￨F which￨F is￨F stored￨F as￨F fat￨F .￨F
The￨F researcher￨F explained￨F that￨F the￨F direct￨F benefit￨F for￨F the￨F participants￨F is￨F a￨F comprehensive￨F assessment￨F of￨F the￨F children￨F ,￨F which￨F can￨F detect￨F if￨F they￨F have￨F any￨F degree￨F of￨F overweight￨F or￨F obesity￨F .￨F
Even￨F ,￨F he￨F said￨F ,￨F the￨F presence￨F of￨F dark-colored￨F folds￨F (acanthuses)￨F on￨F the￨F neck￨F and￨F forearm￨F indicates￨F the￨F likelihood￨F of￨F suffering￨F of￨F metabolic￨F disorders￨F and￨F even￨F prediabetes￨F .￨F
The￨F information￨F is￨F handled￨F with￨F confidentiality￨F ,￨F doctors￨F deliver￨F it￨F in￨F writing￨F to￨F the￨F parents￨F ,￨F to￨F whom￨F they￨F explain￨F each￨F of￨F the￨F measurements￨F and￨F changes￨F in￨F the￨F lifestyle￨F that￨F have￨F to￨F be￨F undertaken￨F in￨F order￨F to￨F prevent￨F disease￨F .￨F
Cruz￨F Lopez￨F explained￨F that￨F there￨F are￨F three￨F major￨F components￨F that￨F cause￨F overweight￨F ,￨F obesity￨F and￨F other￨F chronic￨F diseases:￨F sedentary￨F lifestyle￨F ,￨F which￨F is￨F the￨F lack￨F of￨F daily￨F physical￨F activity￨F ,￨F staying￨F most￨F of￨F the￨F day￨F and￨F watching￨F TV￨F and￨F using￨F means￨F of￨F transport￨F instead￨F of￨F walking￨F short￨F distances￨F .￨F
Also￨F it￨F is￨F due￨F to￨F the￨F high￨F caloric￨F intake￨F ,￨F meaning￨F ,￨F and￨F the￨F increased￨F consumption￨F of￨F sugary￨F drinks￨F ,￨F carbohydrate￨F (tamales￨F ,￨F bread￨F ,￨F pizza￨F ,￨F hamburger￨F ,￨F etc￨F .)￨F with￨F high￨F fat￨F and￨F protein￨F and￨F genetics￨F analyzed￨F in￨F this￨F protocol￨F .￨F
UNAM￨F asphalt￨F would￨F avoid￨F potholes￨F
Rafael￨F Herrera￨F ,￨F a￨F researcher￨F at￨F the￨F Faculty￨F of￨F Chemistry￨F of￨F UNAM￨F ,￨F develops￨F polymer-modified￨F asphalt￨F to￨F produce￨F a￨F mixture￨F with￨F the￨F best￨F performance￨F ,￨F regardless￨F of￨F the￨F environmental￨F conditions￨F and￨F temperature￨F
If￨F the￨F signals￨F sent￨F by￨F the￨F road￨F surface￨F were￨F attended￨F ,￨F it￨F would￨F be￨F necessary￨F to￨F repair￨F about￨F 200￨F thousand￨F potholes￨F every￨F rainy￨F season￨F in￨F the￨F Metropolitan￨F Area￨F of￨F Valley￨F of￨F Mexico￨F ,￨F said￨F Rafael￨F Herrera￨F Najera￨F ,￨F a￨F researcher￨F at￨F the￨F Chemistry￨F Faculty￨F (CF)￨F of￨F the￨F UNAM￨F ,￨F who￨F said￨F that￨F if￨F the￨F process￨F of￨F construction￨F and￨F maintenance￨F of￨F an￨F asphalt￨F pavement￨F is￨F adequate￨F ,￨F the￨F potholes￨F could￨F be￨F reduced￨F or￨F even￨F completely￨F eliminated￨F .￨F
In￨F his￨F lecture￨F A￨F technological￨F view￨F of￨F the￨F pothole￨F ,￨F issued￨F under￨F the￨F International￨F Year￨F of￨F Chemistry￨F ,￨F announced￨F that￨F the￨F laboratory￨F he￨F is￨F responsible￨F for￨F is￨F developing￨F a￨F polymer￨F modified￨F asphalt￨F to￨F produce￨F a￨F mixture￨F with￨F characteristics￨F similar￨F to￨F the￨F asphalt￨F ,￨F but￨F with￨F a￨F better￨F mechanical￨F strength￨F ,￨F both￨F at￨F high￨F and￨F low￨F temperatures￨F .￨F
Herrera￨F Nájera￨F said￨F that￨F this￨F type￨F of￨F modified￨F asphalt￨F could￨F be￨F used￨F in￨F places￨F where￨F the￨F weather￨F is￨F extremely￨F hot￨F ,￨F as￨F some￨F cities￨F in￨F the￨F north￨F ,￨F to￨F improve￨F its￨F performance￨F and￨F ,￨F therefore￨F ,￨F the￨F formation￨F of￨F potholes￨F .￨F
He￨F explained￨F that￨F the￨F asphalt￨F ,￨F the￨F heavier￨F oil￨F part￨F is￨F a￨F set￨F of￨F hydrocarbon￨F molecules￨F ,￨F some￨F of￨F high￨F molecular￨F weight￨F ,￨F called￨F asphaltenes￨F ,￨F and￨F other￨F of￨F low￨F molecular￨F weight￨F ,￨F called￨F maltenes￨F ,￨F which￨F together￨F give￨F the￨F road￨F surface￨F its￨F viscoelastic￨F characteristic￨F behavior￨F .￨F
The￨F viscoelastic￨F behavior￨F of￨F the￨F asphalt￨F consists￨F in￨F the￨F fact￨F that￨F at￨F high￨F temperatures￨F near￨F 180￨F degrees￨F ,￨F it￨F behaves￨F like￨F a￨F liquid￨F at￨F 120￨F °￨F C￨F ,￨F its￨F viscosity￨F is￨F very￨F high￨F and￨F at￨F 50￨F degrees￨F Celsius￨F has￨F a￨F nearly￨F solid￨F state￨F ,￨F whereas￨F at￨F very￨F low￨F temperatures￨F the￨F asphalt￨F becomes￨F fragile￨F ,￨F he￨F said￨F .￨F
This￨F means￨F that￨F the￨F resistance￨F of￨F the￨F street￨F asphalt￨F is￨F not￨F uniform￨F ,￨F but￨F is￨F modified￨F during￨F the￨F day￨F according￨F to￨F the￨F environmental￨F conditions￨F and￨F temperature￨F ,￨F said￨F the￨F specialist￨F in￨F chemical￨F engineering￨F .￨F
CF￨F researcher￨F observed￨F that￨F the￨F streets￨F of￨F Mexico￨F City￨F are￨F mostly￨F covered￨F by￨F flexible￨F pavement￨F ,￨F which￨F is￨F composed￨F of￨F six￨F layers￨F of￨F material￨F ,￨F out￨F of￨F which￨F the￨F last￨F three￨F involve￨F the￨F asphalt￨F .￨F
Among￨F the￨F most￨F superficial￨F layers￨F is￨F the￨F asphalt￨F ,￨F composed￨F of￨F small￨F stones￨F dipped￨F into￨F the￨F asphalt￨F and￨F then￨F compacted￨F .￨F
Each￨F of￨F the￨F stones￨F which￨F compose￨F this￨F covering￨F ,￨F he￨F said￨F ,￨F is￨F dipped￨F with￨F asphalt￨F .￨F
When￨F driving￨F vehicles￨F and￨F generating￨F effort￨F ,￨F it￨F allows￨F the￨F forces￨F to￨F spread￨F very￨F well￨F on￨F the￨F pavement￨F .￨F
If￨F it￨F were￨F modified￨F asphalt￨F it￨F would￨F spread￨F even￨F better￨F ,￨F said￨F the￨F chemical￨F engineer￨F .￨F
On￨F the￨F asphalt￨F covering￨F ,￨F he￨F added￨F ,￨F is￨F placed￨F a￨F final￨F layer￨F called￨F rolling￨F covering￨F ,￨F which￨F is￨F made￨F ​￨F ​￨F of￨F a￨F fine￨F stone￨F material￨F ,￨F meaning￨F sand￨F also￨F dipped￨F into￨F the￨F asphalt￨F .￨F
Since￨F this￨F is￨F the￨F layer￨F that￨F will￨F be￨F in￨F contact￨F with￨F the￨F wheels￨F of￨F the￨F vehicle￨F ,￨F it￨F must￨F have￨F a￨F better￨F mechanical￨F strength￨F than￨F the￨F asphalt￨F covering￨F and￨F provide￨F road￨F friction￨F .￨F
As￨F being￨F the￨F part￨F of￨F the￨F pavement￨F that￨F will￨F receive￨F and￨F diffuse￨F the￨F efforts￨F ,￨F the￨F rolling￨F covering￨F also￨F requires￨F proper￨F thickness￨F and￨F the￨F material￨F it￨F is￨F made￨F of￨F must￨F be￨F take￨F into￨F consideration￨F .￨F
The￨F weather￨F ,￨F especially￨F humidity￨F and￨F temperature￨F variations￨F are￨F also￨F a￨F very￨F important￨F factor￨F to￨F consider￨F ,￨F especially￨F water￨F ,￨F he￨F said￨F ,￨F because￨F it￨F greatly￨F affects￨F the￨F performance￨F of￨F the￨F asphalt￨F .￨F
